	focus = {
		id = ARG_the_second_cisplatine_war_focus
		icon = GFX_ARG_second_cisplatine
		x = 2
		y = 1

		relative_position_id = ARG_have_our_own_territorial_gains
		prerequisite = { focus = ARG_have_our_own_territorial_gains }
		
		
		cost = 5
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}
		
		available = {
			has_war_with = BRA
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = ARG_the_second_cisplatine_war
				has_idea = ARG_the_second_cisplatine_war_2 
			}
		}

		allow_branch = {
			has_country_flag = ARG_is_in_cisplatine_war
		}
		
		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		continue_if_invalid = no
		available_if_capitulated = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT }
		completion_reward = {
			add_war_support = 0.35
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ARG_the_second_cisplatine_war
				add_idea = ARG_the_second_cisplatine_war_2
			}
		}
	}
